     558              : #define UINT16_LOW_BYTE( x )              ( ( uint8_t ) ( ( x ) & 0x00ffU ) )
     559              : 
     560              : /**
     561              :  * @brief Macro for decoding a 2-byte unsigned int from a sequence of bytes.
     562              :  *
     563              :  * @param[in] ptr A uint8_t* that points to the high byte.
     564              :  */
     565              : #define UINT16_DECODE( ptr )                            \
     566              :     ( uint16_t ) ( ( ( ( uint16_t ) ptr[ 0 ] ) << 8 ) | \
     567              :                    ( ( uint16_t ) ptr[ 1 ] ) )
     568              : 
     569              : #if ( MQTT_VERSION_5_ENABLED )
     570              : 
     571              : /**
     572              :  * @brief Get the 4th byte of a 32-bit unsigned integer.
     573              :  */
     574              :     #define UINT32_BYTE3( x )    ( ( uint8_t ) ( ( x ) >> 24 ) )
     575              : 
     576              : /**
     577              :  * @brief Get the 3rd byte of a 32-bit unsigned integer.
     578              :  */
     579              :     #define UINT32_BYTE2( x )    ( ( uint8_t ) ( ( x ) >> 16 ) )
     580              : 
     581              : /**
     582              :  * @brief Get the 2nd byte of a 32-bit unsigned integer.
     583              :  */
     584              :     #define UINT32_BYTE1( x )    ( ( uint8_t ) ( ( x ) >> 8 ) )
     585              : 
     586              : /**
     587              :  * @brief Get the 1st byte of a 32-bit unsigned integer.
     588              :  */
     589              :     #define UINT32_BYTE0( x )    ( ( uint8_t ) ( ( x ) & 0x000000FFU ) )
     590              : 
     591              : /**
     592              :  * @brief Macro for decoding a 4-byte unsigned int from a sequence of bytes.
     593              :  *
     594              :  * @param[in] ptr A uint8_t* that points to the high byte.
     595              :  */
     596              :     #define UINT32_DECODE( ptr )                         \
     597              :     ( uint32_t ) ( ( ( ( uint32_t ) ptr[ 0 ] ) << 24 ) | \
     598              :                    ( ( ( uint32_t ) ptr[ 1 ] ) << 16 ) | \
     599              :                    ( ( ( uint32_t ) ptr[ 2 ] ) << 8 ) |  \
     600              :                    ( ( uint32_t ) ptr[ 3 ] ) )
     601              : 
     602              : #endif /* if ( MQTT_VERSION_5_ENABLED ) */

     609              : #define MQTT_REMAINING_LENGTH_INVALID             ( ( size_t ) 268435456 )

     616              : #define MQTT_MIN_PUBLISH_REMAINING_LENGTH_QOS0    ( 3U )

    1981              : 
    1982           96 :     static MQTTStatus_t decodeVariableLength( const uint8_t * pBuffer,
    1983              :                                               size_t * pLength )
    1984              :     {
    1985           96 :         size_t remainingLength = 0;
    1986           96 :         size_t multiplier = 1;
    1987           96 :         size_t bytesDecoded = 0;
    1988           96 :         size_t expectedSize = 0;
    1989           96 :         uint8_t encodedByte = 0;
    1990           96 :         MQTTStatus_t status = MQTTSuccess;
    1991              : 
    1992              :         /* This algorithm is copied from the MQTT v3.1.1 spec. */
    1993              :         do
    1994              :         {
    1995          130 :             if( multiplier > 2097152U ) /* 128 ^ 3 */
    1996              :             {
    1997            4 :                 remainingLength = MQTT_REMAINING_LENGTH_INVALID;
    1998              : 
    1999            4 :                 LogError( ( "Invalid remaining length in the packet.\n" ) );
    2000              : 
    2001            4 :                 status = MQTTBadResponse;
    2002              :             }
    2003              :             else
    2004              :             {
    2005              :                 /* Get the next byte. It is at the next position after the bytes
    2006              :                  * decoded till now since the header of one byte was read before. */
    2007          126 :                 encodedByte = pBuffer[ bytesDecoded ];
    2008          126 :                 remainingLength += ( ( size_t ) encodedByte & 0x7FU ) * multiplier;
    2009          126 :                 multiplier *= 128U;
    2010          126 :                 bytesDecoded++;
    2011              :             }
    2012              : 
    2013              :             /* If the response is incorrect then
    2014              :              * break out of the loop. */
    2015          130 :             if( remainingLength == MQTT_REMAINING_LENGTH_INVALID )
    2016              :             {
    2017            4 :                 break;
    2018              :             }
    2019          126 :         } while( ( encodedByte & 0x80U ) != 0U );
    2020              : 
    2021           96 :         if( status == MQTTSuccess )
    2022              :         {
    2023              :             /* Check that the decoded remaining length conforms to the MQTT specification. */
    2024           92 :             expectedSize = remainingLengthEncodedSize( remainingLength );
    2025              : 
    2026           92 :             if( bytesDecoded != expectedSize )
    2027              :             {
    2028            4 :                 LogError( ( "Expected and actual length of decoded bytes do not match.\n" ) );
    2029            4 :                 status = MQTTBadResponse;
    2030              :             }
    2031              :             else
    2032              :             {

    2901          914 : static size_t remainingLengthEncodedSize( size_t length )

    2909          914 :     if( length < 128U )

    2916           12 :         encodedSize = 2U;

    2929          914 :     LogDebug( ( "Encoded size for length %lu is %lu bytes.",
